## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population P and time t, which is the core ODE formulation in population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic growth, Allee effects, or time-varying carrying capacities.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth decelerating logarithmically near carrying capacity)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below critical threshold)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (per-capita growth rate increases then decreases)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (density-dependent growth with proportional removal)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant removal rate)
- Time-varying exponential: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (growth rate changing exponentially with time)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (logistic with shifting capacity)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**(c2)) * (c2 + 1) (asymmetric sigmoid growth)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolic vs catabolic scaling)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (higher-order density effects)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (saturating birth rate minus linear death)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear dependence on P (dP_dt ŌłØ P) ŌåÆ exponential/Malthusian dynamics with constant per-capita growth rate
- Quadratic term in P (P┬▓ term) ŌåÆ density-dependent feedback, typically logistic-type self-limitation
- Cubic term in P (P┬│ term) ŌåÆ Allee effect or bistability with two stable equilibria
- Logarithmic coupling log(P) ŌåÆ Gompertz-type growth with multiplicative deceleration near capacity
- Ratio of polynomials in P ŌåÆ saturating functional responses (e.g., Beverton-Holt, Holling type II birth rates)
- Explicit time dependence through multiplicative modulation ŌåÆ seasonality or environmental trends affecting growth parameters
- Difference of power laws (P^a - P^b) ŌåÆ competing metabolic or demographic scaling processes
- Product of multiple linear factors in P ŌåÆ multiple equilibrium points (extinction, Allee threshold, carrying capacity)
- Per-capita growth rate (dP_dt/P) being linear in P ŌåÆ classic logistic; nonlinear in P ŌåÆ generalized density dependence
- Periodic time modulation sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) multiplying growth terms ŌåÆ seasonal forcing of reproduction or mortality
